1 # Copy/Paste of MS950.map
    2 #
    3 # (1)sorted
    4 # (2)added the singlebyte back in
    5 # (3)added the MS950.b2c-irreversible (b2c only table)
    6 #
    7 # This table comes from MS CP950 table posted on unicode.org webpage
    8 # with the modifications of 
    9 #
   10 # (1)removed
   11 #      0x00 - 0x7f
   12 # (2)removed DBCS lead byte entries 
   13 #      0x80 - 0xff  
   14 # (3)added EUDC entries.
   15 #      0xFA40 - 0xFEFE  U+E000 - U+E310  
   16 #      0x8E40 - 0xA0FE  U+E311 - U+EEB7  
   17 #      0x8140 - 0x8DFE  U+EEB8 - U+F6B0  
   18 #      0xC6A1 - 0xC8FE  U+F6B1 - U+F848  
   19 # (4)roundtrip mapping conflicts
   20 #    0xF9FA -> u256D -> 0xA27E 
   21 #    0xF9FB -> u256E -> 0xA2A1 
   22 #    0xF9FC -> u2570 -> 0xA2A2 
   23 #    0xF9FD -> u256F -> 0xA2A3 
   24 #    0xA2CC -> u5341 -> 0xA451 
   25 #    0xA2CE -> u5345 -> 0xA4CA  
   26 #    0xA2A4 -> u2550 -> 0xF9F9
   27 #    0xA2A5 -> u255E -> 0xF9E9
   28 #    0xA2A6 -> u256A -> 0xF9EA
   29 #    0xA2A7 -> u2561 -> 0xF9EB
   30 #
   31 # Column #1 is the cp950 code (in hex)
   32 # Column #2 is the Unicode (in hex as 0xXXXX)
   33 # Column #3 is the Unicode name (follows a comment sign, '#')
   34 #
   35 # The entries are in Unicode order
   36 #
   37 0x00	0x0000
   38 0x01	0x0001
   39 0x02	0x0002
   40 0x03	0x0003
   41 0x04	0x0004
   42 0x05	0x0005
   43 0x06	0x0006
   44 0x07	0x0007
   45 0x08	0x0008
   46 0x09	0x0009
   47 0x0a	0x000a
   48 0x0b	0x000b
   49 0x0c	0x000c
   50 0x0d	0x000d
   51 0x0e	0x000e
   52 0x0f	0x000f
   53 0x10	0x0010
   54 0x11	0x0011
   55 0x12	0x0012
   56 0x13	0x0013
   57 0x14	0x0014
   58 0x15	0x0015
   59 0x16	0x0016
   60 0x17	0x0017
   61 0x18	0x0018
   62 0x19	0x0019
   63 0x1a	0x001a
   64 0x1b	0x001b
   65 0x1c	0x001c
   66 0x1d	0x001d
   67 0x1e	0x001e
   68 0x1f	0x001f
   69 0x20    0x0020  # SPACE
   70 0x21    0x0021  # EXCLAMATION MARK
   71 0x22    0x0022  # QUOTATION MARK
   72 0x23    0x0023  # NUMBER SIGN
   73 0x24    0x0024  # DOLLAR SIGN
   74 0x25    0x0025  # PERCENT SIGN
   75 0x26    0x0026  # AMPERSAND
   76 0x27    0x0027  # APOSTROPHE
   77 0x28    0x0028  # LEFT PARENTHESIS
   78 0x29    0x0029  # RIGHT PARENTHESIS
   79 0x2A    0x002A  # ASTERISK
   80 0x2B    0x002B  # PLUS SIGN
   81 0x2C    0x002C  # COMMA
   82 0x2D    0x002D  # HYPHEN-MINUS
   83 0x2E    0x002E  # FULL STOP
   84 0x2F    0x002F  # SOLIDUS
   85 0x30    0x0030  # DIGIT ZERO
   86 0x31    0x0031  # DIGIT ONE
   87 0x32    0x0032  # DIGIT TWO
   88 0x33    0x0033  # DIGIT THREE
   89 0x34    0x0034  # DIGIT FOUR
